I was referred to Dr Harris by my primary physician, so arrived with high confidence and expectations. Dr. Harris' team was friendly, professional and efficient. My exam/consult was focused and brief, but complete and Dr Harris exuded confidence in my case. The surgery was set 3 weeks out to accommodate my vacation plans. Communication leading to the surgery was consistent and comprehensive. The surgery staff from prep nurse to anesthesiologist to recovery nurse were friendly, informative, professional and reassuring. The surgery was uneventfully positive and the directions for recovery protocol were comprehensive and accurate to guide my recovery completely. Now, 3 weeks post op, I'm pain free and very pleased with the results, both functionally and cosmetically. I heartily recommend Dr Harris if you have a hernia and choose to seek repair.<//review>

< review>
The entire team at California Hernia Specialists is absolutely fantastic.  Mari is exceptionally understanding and accommodating, Itzel is incredibly personable and helpful, and Dr. Harris has to be one of best medical professionals I have ever been served by.  I had an umbilical hernia repair done a little over three weeks ago, and I was astounded by how seamless the recovery was.  I only ever needed to use opioid painkillers once, the very night after the surgery, and it was only at the direction of hospital staff.  A certain amount of soreness set in on the second day, but again, Dr. Harris' expertise and techniques are such that by the third and fourth day, it was almost forgettable that I had even gone in for surgery.  Dr. Harris takes time to field any questions you may have regarding your hernia, the surgery and recovery outlook.  He is kind, caring and has an obvious interest in the best outcome for his patients.  If I were to be given the choice between California Hernia Specialists, and going somewhere else, I would 100% choose Dr. Harris all over again.  I urge anyone and everyone with a hernia to save themselves the trouble of finding another doctor to do their hernia repair, because they're not going to find another team better suited for the job.</review>

< review>
Dr. Todd Harris is an excellent MD and the experience I had was top notch.  I had a bilateral inguinal hernia and originally I had been referred by my primary care physician to a different surgeon.  For multiple reasons I decided to go elswhere and did my own research where I found Dr. Todd Harris with California Hernia Specialists.  My initial appointment with Dr. Harris was about two weeks from when I first contacted his office.  At my initial consultation I had almost no wait time and upon meeting Dr. Harris I found him to be very pleasant and professional.  The consultation was relatively quick (I wasn't expecting a lengthy one) and he described to me what would be done and answered all of my questions.  The staff at Dr. Harris' office looked into my insurance and advised me of costs within a couple/few days.  To my surprise it turned out, in my particular case, that going out of network was actually more cost effective by about 40%.  Not sure of all the details why but some of it had to do that I have an HSA PPO so I definitely saved some dollars there...a big thank you for that one!  Less than two weeks later I had my procedure done laparoscopically at Prime Surgical Center in Newport Beach and the facilities and staff are absoulutely outstanding.  Dr. Harris performed the procedure in a little less than an hour.  My recovery was fast with no significant pain.  What I felt was more like bloated, gas discomfort so I didn't take any pain killers (not even a Tylenol).  However, if I coughed or sneezed, well that's another story.  All I had was the expected swelling/bruising for several days afterward.  At week three I had my follow-up with Dr. Harris where everything went well and was given a detailed summary of what he did during the procedure.  It's been five weeks since the surgery and everything is great and has healed-up nicely.
I highly recommend Dr. Harris, his staff and the staff at Prime Surgical Center in Newport Beach.  Many thanks to all who took part in this for a very efficient procedure!< /review>

<Response>{'time': 1518108449591, 'text': "Nicole,\n\nThank you for the time on the phone yesterday to discuss your experience with my office. I am sorry for the frustration you encountered when trying to have your husband seen. That is clearly not our intention and we usually pride ourselves on being very organized.\n\nAs I mentioned yesterday, when we called to confirm your husbands appointment and to convey the status of your deductible, we received your voicemail instead of his. To avoid any HIPAA violations, we do not typically leave voice messages for patients when we are unsure of the voicemail. However, you are 100% correct in that you told my office that you were the person in charge of scheduling and communications with our office and it is our fault for not documenting that in our electronic chart as we typically do. If we had done so, we likely would have been able to avoid the circumstances which followed. For this, I apologize and our office will do a better job in the future.\n\nAlso as we discussed, I believe there may have been a misunderstanding with regards to our accepting your insurance. We absolutely accept your insurance; however, you have not met any of your deductible which is common with most of our patients at this point early in the year. Because of this, we are required to collect the amount allowed by your insurance for a consultation which is approximately $250. <Rating>5< /Rating>< Review>
Commendation for Dr. Manjunath Vadmal

Dr. Vadmal MD. PhD. has been my dermatologist of long standing and whom I see four times a year for regular check ups. My recent visit was once again an occasion for complete satisfaction for (1) the highly skilled care which Dr. Vadmal rendered to me, along with (2) the outstanding courteous service provided by the entire Skin and Beauty Center staff of well trained nursed, medical assistants, and the attendants who take care of the checking in process, insurance matters, payments and scheduling.

Dr. Vadmal's clinical diagnoses, evaluations, assessments and treatments are grounded and informed by an outstanding educational background in the life sciences augmented by continuous ongoing study and a broad and extensive practical knowledge and skill in surgical techniques. Dr. Vadmal brings to the care of each of his patients an empathetic understanding of their personal concerns about their health; his calm and collected state of being, gentle strength and soft spoken manner provides reassurance, and is conducive for the alleviation anxiety and apprehensiveness that patients may have as regards their conditions and curative medical procedures.

I recommend Dr, Vadmal without reservation to anyone who is seeking to receive the very finest professional care for their dermatological needs and the achievement and maintenance of optimal health for their skin.

Steven Konstantine 03/06/18

Burbank CA</Review>

< pictures>
[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNVB7cjwh2Yc8S3j9R3yCFa-yzFsk64scxmUUxv=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPWSp2ki1IQYeSxFi5YNfd4XMVGuAWUlJ_80y_O=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPhgPEu__6SicBm-cqZz2fmWA0E-0sDeBr-EPJZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN7Q0rGKqgqRGslPngnckJ7_u5mbOIznT1Uslqg=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOyQp8TcNXko_D_25dVLyhMRsRtzgxStYxofn_M=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNA-90oOn1zrBn4bwUnjxLMR_-qzDkXRSnb0EHm=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMoKlPMMmXQSKtOYoz-bhVWFwYoNiHupMqxq92Y=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pictures>
<Text>I stopped by here for lunch with my dog, Charlie, on a Saturday.  There was plenty of outdoor seating and the outdoor seating is situated like most of the restaurant on University Ave.  I ordered their shrimp spring roll, grilled chicken banh mi and their walking chicken pho.

I tasted the pho broth immediately and initial thoughts was that it's light, a little less flavor than I would like but I still liked it.  The shredded chicken pieces are one of the most tender and succulent I've had at any pho restaurants.  I normally get dried tasting chicken pieces in other pho restaurants.  They also offer a chicken pho for $2 less.

The spring rolls was also good and looks like it was made to order.  The peanut sauce is on par with other pho restaurants.

I only ate half of the grilled banh me sandwich mostly because I was getting full but I still enjoyed it.  The baggutte was soft and warm, you get pieces of chicken, cilantro, pickled radish and carrot with every bite.

Now the prices.  I see a fair number of complaint about the price and how they can get it cheaper and better elsewhere .  That's probably the case in most instances but you should have known that going into this restaurant.  I knew the prices and still wanted to try it and it was a good meal.  It more than what I would typically pay for banh mi and a bowl of pho but I didn't let that hinder my experience.  The staff were nice, attentive and brought water immediately.  I can't also take Charlie with me to a vast majority of pho restaurants so I really like that aspect of Pho Banh Mi also.

Total bill was around $48 with taxes and tips.</Text>< rating>
4< /rating>

<review>The food was all very delicious, and the decor and atmosphere were super pleasant, too. I ordered the Pho Seafood, which was full of all kinds of delicious and fresh fish, and had just enough spice to both have a satisfying kick but not take away from any of the flavor. My mom and I split a Banh Mi combo, and were pleasantly surprised to find the meats perfectly balanced with the sweet and crunchy veggies. The Rancho Special tea was perfectly sweet and had really soft boba pearls, as well, which was great because not many restaurants have good food and boba. My mom enjoyed her vermicelli and combo spring rolls, too! Shout out to our host Billy, who was really kind and friendly and explained everything for us perfectly. Would recommend to anyone looking for good Vietnamese food in Palo Alto! :)</review>< Pictures>

I'm always willing to give feedback and I try to make it worthwhile to the organization requesting it...not just a lazy "10" and a lot of platitudes...that doesn't offer anything substantive and also reflect my belief that we all, certainly my work, can do better.  I'm going to give the less than satisfied first but obviously from giving 4 out of 5 stars, the pro's dominate...

Context: I have had my house on the market, using Zillow, networking and no agent, twice in the last year, last fall at $12,500 then $11,500...and then again starting in April dropping from $11,500 to $10,500. At each of these levels I showed the house to multiple prospective renters getting one offer at $9,500 and a short term offer last year at a premium (but didn't entertain or even ask for a number).  We were informed by professionals (friends in RE) that the market was softening.  Our objective was to rent it for one year, open to a two year lease. Then we received interest from a short term (4 month lease) prospect and we  accepted them as renters because, 1) because of a premium ($3000) over asking and, 2) they took it totally furnished with added flexibility on what we could leave in the house. I should add that they are local and well established in the community.  So why the 4 stars? Victor stepped up, not only in general about being responsive to the urgency to get this done on by the prospective tenants and our request, but in handling numerous last minute changes on the lease by the prospective tenants. What I perceived as needing to nudge Victor was, in retrospect, my having managed the process so not allowing fully for not only his having more than just us as a clients but also a rigorous (sometimes to a fault) process to adhere to. In the end I don't hesitate to give Victor his due, he came through like a champ.
A final, somewhat indulgent and non-substantive comment which I already expressed to Victor and admittedly just one person's opinion: the voice that answers the phone when I call Victor's direct line is...somewhere between very hard to listen to and...awful. Unfortunately, when making the sandwiches (2), she grabbed jalepenos then put the same gloved hand into the olives.
I do not like hot food. So when she made mine she must have dipped her hand in the vegetables and mixed them up. When i took it home, i started to eat it and i could taste the jalepenos throughout my sandwich.
